\DoxyCodeLine{2310   \textcolor{comment}{// ES6 13.7.4.8 specifies that on each loop iteration the let variables are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2311   \textcolor{comment}{// copied into a new environment.  Moreover, the "{}next"{} statement must be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2312   \textcolor{comment}{// evaluated not in the environment of the just completed iteration but in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2313   \textcolor{comment}{// that of the upcoming one.  We achieve this with the following desugaring.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2314   \textcolor{comment}{// Extra care is needed to preserve the completion value of the original loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2315   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2316   \textcolor{comment}{// We are given a for statement of the form}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2317   \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2319   \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2322   \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2726   \textcolor{comment}{// We can only parse lazily if we also compile lazily. The heuristics for lazy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2727   \textcolor{comment}{// compilation are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728   \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ It must not have been prohibited by the caller to Parse (some callers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729   \textcolor{comment}{//   need a full AST).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730   \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The outer scope must allow lazy compilation of inner functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731   \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The function mustn't be a function expression with an open parenthesis}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2732   \textcolor{comment}{//   before; we consider that a hint that the function will be called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733   \textcolor{comment}{//   immediately, and it would be a waste of time to make it lazily}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2734   \textcolor{comment}{//   compiled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2735   \textcolor{comment}{// These are all things we can know at this point, without looking at the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2737 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2738   \textcolor{comment}{// We separate between lazy parsing top level functions and lazy parsing inner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739   \textcolor{comment}{// functions, because the latter needs to do more work. In particular, we need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740   \textcolor{comment}{// to track unresolved variables to distinguish between these cases:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2741   \textcolor{comment}{// (function foo() \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742   \textcolor{comment}{//   bar = function() \{ return 1; \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2743   \textcolor{comment}{//  \})();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744   \textcolor{comment}{// and}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2747   \textcolor{comment}{//   bar = function() \{ return a; \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2748   \textcolor{comment}{//  \})();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2750   \textcolor{comment}{// Now foo will be parsed eagerly and compiled eagerly (optimization: assume}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2753   \textcolor{comment}{// that tracks unresolved variables.}}
